# Stack Protection Mechanisms in LLVM

## Your Task

Find all C++ source files in `llvm/llvm-project` that implement stack protection mechanisms against buffer overflow attacks. Specifically identify: 1. The LLVM pass that inserts stack protector checks (look for `StackProtector` in `llvm/lib/CodeGen/`). 2. The file that defines the `SafeStack` pass that separates safe and unsafe stack allocations (under `llvm/lib/CodeGen/`). 3. The header file that declares the stack protection pass interface. 4. The compiler-rt runtime file that provides the `__stack_chk_fail` implementation (look under `compiler-rt/lib/builtins/`). 5. Any file in `llvm/lib/Transforms/Instrumentation/` that implements memory safety instrumentation related to stack frame protection. Report the repo, file path, and the primary function or class handling stack protection for each.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the security domain.

## Available Resources

No local repositories are pre-checked out.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `github.com/llvm/llvm-project` (llvm/llvm-project)
- `github.com/gcc-mirror/gcc` (gcc-mirror/gcc)

Perfect! I've completed a comprehensive analysis of the stack protection mechanisms in the LLVM project. Here's what I found:

## Summary of Stack Protection Files Found

I identified **10 key C++ source files** implementing stack protection mechanisms in LLVM:

### Core Stack Protection Components:

1. **StackProtector Pass** (`llvm/lib/CodeGen/StackProtector.cpp`)
   - Inserts stack canary checks in function prologue/epilogue
   - Key functions: `InsertStackProtectors()`, `CreateFailBB()`
   - Implements classic stack guard protection

2. **StackProtector Header** (`llvm/include/llvm/CodeGen/StackProtector.h`)
   - Declares pass interfaces for both legacy and new pass managers
   - Contains `SSPLayoutAnalysis`, `StackProtectorPass`, and `StackProtector` classes

3. **SafeStack Pass** (`llvm/lib/CodeGen/SafeStack.cpp`)
   - Separates safe/unsafe stack allocations
   - Contains `checkStackGuard()` for verifying stack integrity
   - Also includes legacy and new pass manager interfaces

4. **SafeStack Headers** (`llvm/include/llvm/CodeGen/SafeStack.h`)
   - Declares SafeStackPass interface

5. **SafeStack Layout Components**
   - `llvm/lib/CodeGen/SafeStackLayout.h` - Layout computation header
   - `llvm/lib/CodeGen/SafeStackLayout.cpp` - Layout implementation

### Runtime Implementation:

6. **Stack Check Fail Runtime** (`libc/src/compiler/generic/__stack_chk_fail.cpp`)
   - Implements `__stack_chk_fail()` - called when stack overflow detected
   - Prints error message and terminates the program
   - Initializes `__stack_chk_guard` with random value (0xa9fff01234)

7. **Stack Check Header** (`libc/src/compiler/__stack_chk_fail.h`)

### Memory Safety Instrumentation:

8. **AddressSanitizer** (`llvm/lib/Transforms/Instrumentation/AddressSanitizer.cpp`)
   - Detects heap/st

It calls __stack_chk_fail if they differ.\n72: static bool InsertStackProtectors(const TargetLowering &TLI,\n73:                                   const LibcallLoweringInfo &Libcalls,\n74:                                   Function *F, DomTreeUpdater *DTU,\n75:                                   bool &HasPrologue, bool &HasIRCheck);\n76: \n77: /// CreateFailBB - Create a basic block to jump to when the stack protector\n78: /// check fails.\n79: static BasicBlock *CreateFailBB(Function *F,\n80:                                 const LibcallLoweringInfo &Libcalls);\n81: \n82: bool SSPLayoutInfo::shouldEmitSDCheck(const BasicBlock &BB) const {\n83:   return HasPrologue && !HasIRCheck && isa<ReturnInst>(BB.getTerminator());\n84: }\n85: \n86: void SSPLayoutInfo::copyToMachineFrameInfo(MachineFrameInfo &MFI) const {\n87:   if (Layout.empty())\n88:     return;\n89: \n90:   for (int I = 0, E = MFI.getObjectIndexEnd(); I != E; ++I) {\n91:     if (MFI.isDeadObjectIndex(I))\n92:       continue;\n93: \n94:     const AllocaInst *AI = MFI.getObjectAllocation(I);\n95:     if (!AI)\n96:       continue;\n97: \n98:     SSPLayoutMap::const_iterator LI = Layout.find(AI);\n99:     if (LI == Layout.end())\n100:       continue;\n101: ",

in LLVM Project\\n\\nThe LLVM/Clang project implements comprehensive stack protection mechanisms against buffer overflow attacks across multiple layers:\\n\\n### 1. StackProtector Pass (llvm/lib/CodeGen/StackProtector.cpp)\\nThis is the primary LLVM pass responsible for inserting stack protector checks. The pass implements the classic stack canary defense mechanism:\\n- **StackProtector class**: A FunctionPass (legacy interface) that inserts stack protectors into functions needing protection\\n- **StackProtectorPass class**: The new pass manager interface for the same functionality\\n- **SSPLayoutAnalysis class**: Analyzes which allocations require stack protection and determines the layout\\n- **InsertStackProtectors()**: Core function that inserts prologue code to load the stack guard value and epilogue code to check it, calling __stack_chk_fail if the guard is corrupted\\n- **CreateFailBB()**: Creates the failure basic block that calls __stack_chk_fail when a stack overflow is detected\\n\\nThe pass loads a random guard value, stores it on the stack before local variables, and checks it upon function exit. If modified, it calls the runtime failure handler.\\n\\n### 2. StackProtector Header (llvm/include/llvm/CodeGen/StackProtector.h)\\nDeclares the pass interface with:\\n- **SSPLayoutInfo struct**: Contains SSP layout mapping and configuration\\n- **StackProtector class**: Legacy pass interface\\n- **StackProtectorPass class**: New pass manager interface\\n- Methods to determine which functions require stack protection based on language level settings\\n\\n### 3. SafeStack Pass (llvm/lib/CodeGen/SafeStack.cpp)\\nImplements a more sophisticated stack protection mechanism that separates safe and unsafe stack allocations:\\n- **SafeStack class**: Implements the core transformation that splits stack into safe (kept in normal stack) and unsafe (explicitly allocated/managed through runtime) regions\\n- **SafeStackPass class**: New pass manager interface\\n- **SafeStackLegacyPass class**: Legacy interface\\n- **checkStackGuard()**: Verifies the stack guard at function return points by comparing stored value against current guard\\n- The pass identifies unsafe allocations (large buffers, variable-sized arrays, objects whose address is taken) and moves them to a separate unsafe stack managed by the safestack runtime library\\n\\n### 4. SafeStack Headers and Layout (llvm/include/llvm/CodeGen/SafeStack.h, llvm/lib/CodeGen/SafeStackLayout.h)\\n- **SafeStackPass**: Declares the pass interface with TargetMachine parameter\\n- **StackLayout class**: Computes memory layout for unsafe stack frames, computing offsets and alignments for stack objects with coloring optimization\\n- Uses **SafeStackLayout.cpp** for layout computation with proper alignment and lifetime analysis\\n\\n### 5. Stack Check Failure Runtime (libc/src/compiler/generic/__stack_chk_fail.cpp)\\nProvides the runtime implementation called when stack overflow is detected:\\n- **__stack_chk_fail()**: Prints \\\"stack smashing detected\\\" message and calls abort() to terminate the program\\n- **__stack_chk_guard**: Global variable initialized with a random value (0xa9fff01234) that serves as the canary\\n- Header declaration in **libc/src/compiler/__stack_chk_fail.h** with noreturn attribute\\n\\n### 6. Memory Safety Instrumentation (llvm/lib/Transforms/Instrumentation/)\\nAdditional memory safety instrumentation passes:\\n- **AddressSanitizer.cpp**: Instruments memory accesses to detect heap/global/stack buffer overflows, use-after-free, and other memory errors\\n- **HWAddressSanitizer.cpp**: Hardware-assisted address sanitizer using tagged addressing for memory error detection\\n\\nThese sanitizers complement stack protectors by detecting various memory safety violations dynamically at runtime.\\n\\n### Integration\\nThe StackProtector pass inserts checks in the IR (StackProtector.cpp:InsertStackProtectors), which is either handled by SelectionDAG (for some targets) or by SafeStack for more comprehensive protection. SafeStack's checkStackGuard() method provides additional runtime verification. When a violation is detected via any mechanism, __stack_chk_fail() is called to terminate the process safely.\\n\"\n}\n",

StackProtector Pass (llvm/lib/CodeGen/StackProtector.cpp)\\nThis is the primary LLVM pass responsible for inserting stack protector checks. The pass implements the classic stack canary defense mechanism:\\n- **StackProtector class**: A FunctionPass (legacy interface) that inserts stack protectors into functions needing protection\\n- **StackProtectorPass class**: The new pass manager interface for the same functionality\\n- **SSPLayoutAnalysis class**: Analyzes which allocations require stack protection and determines the layout\\n- **InsertStackProtectors()**: Core function that inserts prologue code to load the stack guard value and epilogue code to check it, calling __stack_chk_fail if the guard is corrupted\\n- **CreateFailBB()**: Creates the failure basic block that calls __stack_chk_fail when a stack overflow is detected\\n\\nThe pass loads a random guard value, stores it on the stack before local variables, and checks it upon function exit.
